<Content>WHAT A BIG MISTAKE!!!!!! I just returned from my vacation from Punta Cana, Dominican Republic and stayed at the Barcelo Bavaro Resorts. This resort actually has 5 different hotels. After much prodding by my travel agent I booked a trip for myself a family member and 2 friends to stay at the Barcelo Bavaro Caribe hotel for 7 days ...WHAT A BIG MISTAKE. Upon arrival to the CARIBE, we found that the lobbies decor was a bit outdated and in need of an overhall. When checking in I had asked if I could get room upgrades (suggested by my travel agent) for my party and was flatly told NO! by the staff. I was a taken aback, not by the response, but how it was said and without any explanation. Without questioning or prodding I accepted my key and was taken to my room with whom I shared with my cousin. Upon enterning the room the first thing that hit me was the musty smell, but I was prepared and had incense to combat this. The next thing that I noticed was that the ceiling was caving in and that there was a leak coming from the same area where the air conditioning unit was located. I immediately called the front desk and told them about the problem and expressed to them that I wanted a room change. I was told to hold off and someone would come to see about the problem. I really did not want to stay in this particular room and requested to speak to a manager or someone in charge. I was then put on hold. When I finally spoke to the manager I told him of the problem and that I wanted a room change, I was told that the reason for the leak was due to the condensation in the room from the air conditioning unit not being turned on, and again was told that someone would be there to see about the problem but no mention of my room being changed. I didn't want to seem as if I was being un-cooperative so I agreed for someone to come and see about the problem. Upon further checking of the room I then discovered that there was a flood in the bathroom, I again called the front desk and expressed to them that because of the room conditions I definitely wanted a room change. Can you believe that they refused to change my room, and told me that a techinician would be there to fix the problem. At this point I was so frustrated not only because of not being accomodated as a guest of this hotelbut by their lack of co-operation. I felt that I should not have had to be incovenienced in this manner. What could I do? I was in a foreign country and couldn't afford to make any other arrangements. I decided to try to make the best of a bad situation and went to the bar because this definitely drove me to drink After about 2 hours I returned to my room to place a call to the states to speak to my travel agent, but prior to placing the call I checked to see if the bathroom flood issue had been taken care of. TO MY SUPRISE THE FLOOD WAS STILL THERE! To make a long story short and beleive me I could go on, my travel agent had to call the hotel and FINALLY, FINALLY I was able to get a room change ....TO ONE OF THE OTHER HOTELS! in the resort. My entire party was moved to the Barcelo Bavaro Beach and we got 2 clean rooms without any musty smells, leaks or floods. This hotel was like night and day from their affiliate hotel the CARIBE. The staff was very cordial and accomodating. I must say for these hotels to be all in the same resort, there is a big difference with customer service! I do understand that the staff works long hours and wear many hats, but I really don't feel I was asking for much. Please if you do book a hotel do not make it the CARIBE!

Unless your flashing a five dollar bill your made of glass. No one cares about your concerns or any issues. Anytime I had a question or concern i felt like I was bothering them. That's insane and every where you go the exchange rate varies....In the restaurants the table linens were always filthy. We had big group with us, I had another friends bring her entire family and we often ate together at the same table every day and I would find food that my one year threw on the floor during breakfast still there at dinner time. It was disgusting and then people wonder why there are so many bugs all over the place. All in all if it wasn't for the beautiful beach or the semi clean pools we would of probably packed up and gone home. From getting so very sick and dealing with the attitude and uncleanliness I would have to say next time I want to see Palm trees and beautiful beaches I will go to my native Puerto Rico or the Bahamas!

<Author>skat94
<Content>Had a great time, loved the beach, the rooms need work My husband and I stayed here for a March getaway. After reading the reviews here I was prepared for a hotel with a great beach, not very good food, and rooms that were old and outdated. I got pretty much what I expected. We had a wonderful time - we relaxed on the beach, gambled at the casino, played miniature golf, and went dancing at the discos. The rooms are outdated and dark but ours did have a very nice balcony. The food is okay. We liked the calimari on the beach at La Uva, and the pizza was very good also. Some of the buffets were better than others (I thought the golf and casino buffets were the best). Most of the staff is very nice (our housekeeper was the sweetest woman) but there were one or two rude workers also. I would recommend this hotel to anyone who is willing to sacrifice room quality for price. I also think it would be good for families because there is a lot to do within this complex. I would not recommend this hotel if you are very sensitive to cigarette smoke (there are a lot of smokers at this hotel), require a more comfortable room, or are a picky eater.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great Vacation For Me...Maybe Not For Others My wife, one-year-old son, and I spent 6 days at the Caribe Hotel in the Barcelo resort. It is absolutely beautiful. Barcelo keeps the gardens well maintained and clean. The room was slightly above average, but I have no reason to complain about it. The two double beds were pushed together to make one huge bed and that was great for us. There's a mini-fridge in the room with complimentary beverages in the room. If you drink a Coke, the next day another Coke will be placed in the fridge. Beer is also in the fridge. Our mini-fridge worked most of the time, but sometimes it didn't. However, free drinks are availble all around the resort so we weren't exactly dying of thirst. Sometimes you have to wait a while for the elevator because there are four floors and the elevator is small. The beach is breathtaking. There are lots of things you can do in the ocean as well like boat rides, jet-skiing, parasailing, etc. The food is wonderful and the buffet restaurants always have different options from day to day and meal to meal. Dominican food is sometimes heavily seasoned, but it tastes great. Some people have complained about having stomach problems because of the food. Personally, I don't think it's the food, but rather the water. Bottled water is available anywhere for free, but I think the juices at the restaurants are probably not made from filtered water; thus, leading to stomach problems. The pools are very nice. There's a baby pool too. The gift shops are over-priced. You can find the same things at 50 to 75% off at the flea market. To get there, go to the Palace Hotel in the resort. Next walk to the beach. Finally, take a left and just short walk away is the flea market. However, everyone will try to get you to buy things in their store. Taxis are a little expensive ($20 USD) from the resort to the airport. When we travel to different countries we always want to learn about the culture. So, we decided to take a taxi to the nearest city, Higuey. We enjoyed our little trip to Higuey because we saw what the houses are like and we saw everyday stores, etc. However, our taxi driver told us that it's not a good idea for a tourist to just wander around Higuey by theirself. A marine park is located near the resort. It's called Manati. We didn't go, but we really wanted to. The only major problem we had was the service at a beach side restaurant called La Uva. The line to be seated was horrible. On two seperate occasions we waited over an hour to be seated. Both times we had to over half an hour to get our glasses filled with water. After that it was another half hour wait for them to take hour order and another half hour for our food to arrive. The food in La Uva is great, but the service is horrendous. Moreover, the plates in the a la carte restaurants are small. So order two or three. But, the plates in the steak house are big...so order one or two. It appeared to me that Dominican's LOVE babies. Our son got first class treatment wherever we went. He was hugged and held and was given a personal tour of the gift shop. In other reviews people have complained and I saw some of those things as well, but not to the degree that others saw them. We speak fluent Spanish, so communicating with the staff was not a problem. However, if you don't speak fluent Spanish, I suggest learning at least the most useful phrases before going. Most of the staff does speak a little English though.  
<Date>Jul 10, 2006

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Stay Away....Stay Very, Very Far Away May 18 - May 21, 2006There is no doubt that the beach and the palm trees are breath-taking. I NOW know that between May and November it is impossibly hot and humid ALL the time. These months are not the months to visit Dom Rep. The accomodations were dreadful. Hours to check in to a dirty mildew smelling room where everything was swollen with the humidity - cracks in the bathroom countertop, slider doors that didn't work, broken lawn furniture on the balcony, broken, chipped everything. The a/c made the room cool, but did nothing to rid it of the humidity. I also had a visitor - a big black roach. Not only was the staff disinterested in providing any service, but they bordered on rude even with an American dollar in view. The place was mobbed on Saturday - the staff made no effort to pick up the garbage laying around. The food was mediocre at best (altho the Casino buffet was very nice) - and I assume all inclusive may mean no one rushes to get you a drink or to make sure it even has alcohol in it. Too many other beautiful beaches to ever return to this particular resort in the Dominican Republic.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Rats at the Barcelo Bavaro Beach/Caribe Resort From Saturday, March 25 through Saturday, April 1 we vacationed in Punta Cana, Dominican Republic, and stayed at the Barcelo Bavaro Beach/Caribe Resort. On two separate occassions we were provided rooms which had rats and do not recommend others stay at this hotel. At 11:00 pm on Wednesday, March 29, we saw a rat run from under the beds. We immediately called the front desk who sent housekeeping to our room and their solution was to spray poison in our room to kill the rat. This was unacceptable to us considering we had a 23 month old son sleeping on a Pack-n-Play near to the floor and I was 21 weeks pregnant. Instead, we asked to move to another room. So, at 11:00 pm, we drug our sleeping child and all of our belongings from one room to another.Two nights later, in our new room, we were awakened at 4:00 am to the sound of a rat chewing on a plastic bag on the top of the bed next to us. When we flipped on the light we saw the rat run from under the beds. We immediately grabbed our sleeping child and brought him into bed with us to get him up from near the ground. Because it was 4:00 in the morning, and we were flying out the next day, we decided not to try and change rooms and disrupt what little sleep we were going to get at that point. We were exhausted for our trip home the next day.We reported both incidents to the hotel while we were there, but no action was taken or extra accommodation made. So, we reported the incident to our booking company once we returned to the U.S. and wrote a letter of complaint. The hotel's response was that the maintenance personnel had checked our room but nothing was found. This was not surprising considering rats don't usually wait around for everyone to arrive. The hotel also said that the rooms had been occupied before and after we left and that no rats have been seen since. Essentially, because they haven't had any other problems in these two rooms, our rats didn't exist.Our letter to the hotel requested three nights reimbursement for the portion of our trip which was disrupted because of the rats. The hotel's response was to offer us a special discount, ocean-front room and VIP treatment next time we come there. Considering they didn't improve our accommodations when we were actually at the hotel, I don't see any reason to believe they would provide us a better vacation a second time around and have no desire to stay at the same hotel. I would highly recommend against staying at this resort.

<Author>bcba
<Content>LOVED the Barcelo Bavaro Beach Complex I spent May 21st-28th, 2006 at the Barcelo Bavaro Beach Caribe Hotel, with my husband and 2 children, ages 14 and 6. This is a beautiful complex of 5 different hotels and you can walk to each or take the tram and go to the various restaurants and bars. We had an excellent time and it's hard to imagine why some people would give this resort and its fabulous staff lousy reviews.ROOM: It was fine! a little musty smelling, but perfectly clean and comfortable. The ceiling above the shower did start leaking. We called the desk, they spoke English, and moved us immediately to another room in the same bldg. A little inconvenient, but not a big deal. The new room was in an even better location. As far as check-in and check-out were concerned, we had no problems at either end and a very short wait time. I think it definitely depends on what day/time you arrive/depart. We arrived at 5 pm on Sunday and checked out at 12 pm the next Sunday.FOOD: Not the best, but I had read lots of reviews from several resorts in Punta Cana and frankly, I didn't expect it to be that great. The best food I found was at La Uva, the seafood lunch grill right on the beach - the calamari, grilled lobster, and fish of the day was good, french fries are good also, and at the Steakhouse - the steak and baked potato was great. They have pizza windows, where you can pick up individual pizzas outside of and during lunch/dinner hours. These are good. You can also order the pizza at all of the restaurants. I thought the Mexican restaurant was quite bad. We only ate there once. We tried the Italian once - I just had a pizza to be safe. My son ordered some type of pasta, which he did not like. The Steakhouse was definitely the best for dinner. The buffets were ok for breakfast. I avoided most of the meats. I tended to stay away from the fresh fruit as well as the cold salads at the buffets. I was just too nervous about the water they were washed with. I ate boiled eggs and cake/bread for breakfast. The bacon was ok. The coffee and cappucinos were delicious! I did not get sick from the food - I was cautious about what I ate. Despite the quality of the food (which is probably a result of it being different from I'm used to as well as the fact that it is prepared in mass quantities), I would go back to this resort in a heartbeat! As for drinks, I loved the Presidente beer. They did put alcohol in all the drinks. Not sure what people are talking about when they say you have to ask for it. I watched as they made them and they put alcohol in every time. I had better luck with drinks when I ordered them off the drink menu. For example, I ordered a margarita (not on the menu) and it tasted like a martini with salt around the glass - nothing like a margarita! Some of the drinks on the menu were great, however. The banana daquiris were quite good, but not always consistent in how they were made from bar to bar.STAFF: Absolutely beautiful people who were warm and friendly as well as service oriented. We tried to speak as much Spanish as we could. The staff loved it when my 6 yr. old daughter attempted to speak Spanish. Many of them seemed to love children. The reviews that mention the rudeness of staff - I have to wonder if it is more a result of the language barrier. When you're in a Spanish-speaking country, you can't expect everyone to speak English! Several of them tried. Their English was certainly better than my Spanish and I appeciated their patience with me. I took a small phrasebook and referred to it a few times, such as when I needed to leave a note asking for 4 toallas (towels) since they only provided 2 the first day. I left 2 dollars, wrote Hola and Gracias and drew a smiley face and always got whatever I asked for - extra pillows, towels, etc. The animation crew were great. Very entertaining. I saw the Tropicallisimo show and one at the Caribe. They were enjoyable, Vegas-type shows. So what if they spoke Spanish and I didn't understand. The music was fun to listen to and the dancers were fun to watch. I'm not sure why people expect Broadway shows in Punta Cana! There were plenty of guards around the complex. They were always in the background and unassuming, but I always felt very safe.BEACH/ WATER ACTIVITIES:Beautiful white sand and blue water- just look at the photos on this site! It is breathtaking. The pools and grounds are absolutely gorgeous as well. You truly feel like you're on Fantasy Island. Yes, there were lots of topless women. You get used to it. My 14 yr. old son was not flipping out about it. It became rather blase. My son went waterskiiing ($25 for 30 min. or $55 with a lesson). We got pulled behind a speedboat on an Island Hopper- it was a large vinyl air-filled tube that you sat on - LOADS of fun and only $8 a person. We went snorkeling in the Coral Reef. Absolutely fabulous trip - a ride on a catamaran out to the reef and 1 hour of snorkeling - only $25 per person. We then bought the DVD of the trip - $40 and worth it. We didn't take any of the more expensive excursions away from the resort. We found we had plenty to do right there and really did not want to spend 3 to 400 dollars for a one day trip. We also used the waterpark - it was a collection of trampolines and small climbing mountains and slides - it looked and sounded a lot more fun than it actually was, however. I LOVED this resort and the people. I would go back next week!

<Author>ca_yee
<Content>Ups and Downs I just returned from a 5 night 6 day vacation at the Barcelo Bavaro Beach Complex. I say the Barcelo Bavaro Beach Complex because, when I booked with Expedia, my itinerary said the Barcelo Bavaro Beach Hotel. Our flight to Punta Cana was fine. Once you get off the plane, when you walk into the airport, they take a picture of you with a couple of locals. Then they make you pay for a tourist card for 10 bucks that you turn around and give right back to them right after you go through immigration. Still not sure why we needed the card instead of just paying 10 bucks and be done with that. Was able to find the Hotelbeds representative that was taking my party of 9 to the complex. There seemed to be some minor mixup at the amount of people they were expecting in my party, which on their paper said there were only 5 of us. Fortunately, I had the paperwork to prove there were 9 of us. Not a bunch of hassle there which was nice and we were on our way. This was our second trip to DR. The first was to Puerto Plata.Got to the complex and attempted to check in. What a fiasco that was. Not sure what the issue was. They had us fill out registration cards and then took my printed documentation for the rooms I had reserved. About 45 minutes of waiting and waiting, the guy came out and said we didn't have a reservation there with the Beach Hotel as my paperwork stated but with the Caribe. Then proceeded to tell us that we are at their mercy on where they placed us because they have an agreement with Expedia to put the guest in any resort that is able to take us. I started to get upset about this but then realized that was not going to do anyone any good. I didn't want to start my vacation off the wrong way so we waited to be shown where the Caribe Hotel was. Waited over 1/2 hr for someone to show us where to go, then my sister calls over a bellhop and says, Caribe and he said se. Then showed us where to go. Finally getting to the reception desk at the Caribe hotel, it then took another 2 hours for them to figure out my reservations. I guess if we would have came up separately, they may have been able to handle the following one one reservation there were 4 people reserved 2 rooms. Then on another receipt, I had my nephew and his girlfriend which reserved 1 room. Then on the last piece of paper, had my neice, other nephew and a friend for 1 more room. Well, I am not sure why this checking in 9 people at once became some humungous issue for them because they sent out 4 different people who all asked me the same question, of how many rooms we reserved. Each time the same question, each time the same answer, 4 rooms. But they seemed to be very confused with this. Not sure why. We stood and sat there hot, hungry, and very agitated for 2 hours. No one could go get anything to eat or drink this entire time. Finally after 2 hours and I think the manager, they finally figured out that we reserved 4 rooms and not 3 rooms. Go figure. They handed us our room cards and that was about it. No information about restaurants, no towel cards. During this whole ordeal I did not make a stink or yell or fuss. I knew that making a scene would be useless so I went with the flow and tried to be patient. Finally get checked into our rooms. 6336 has a moldy smell to it. 6340 did not have any odd smells but had small buggies crawling all over the credenza. 6341 had some type of bed bugs that bit my nephews girlfriends legs up pretty good. We only know this because they moved to the other double bed and lo and behold she didn't have anymore mysterious bites the rest of the trip. 6346 had a minor smell to it the safe did not work, the front of the panel was gone. But we all brought candles or plug-ins to make the rooms smell better if we didn't like the smell. The air conditioners in all the units worked well. Actually, they were very powerful and I got cold in the middle of the night. The rooms are a bit dated but it served it's purpose. None of us got any face towels. After hunting down my 5th maid, finally found one! Luckily, they left me that one for the rest of the week. Usually had our towels replaced but one day we didn't get hand towels or the towel for the floor. No big deal, just didn't step out of the shower with wet feet or you'll be taking a ride like my other sister did. Used the safe in the room, found that you don't need to swipe your credit card. The only thing that concerned me is that if for some odd reason if someone put their room number in for their passcode in the safe, anyone could get into the safe. Because they would be able to unlock and relock your safe without you knowing it. The only thing that bothered me is that anyone could go to your room press Clear wait then put a new code in to unlock the safe and take your stuff and then re-lock it and then you are screwed. But, I guess you have to have faith in people. Fortunately, nothing happened to our belongings that were placed in the safe. We left tips every day but that didn't garner us any extra towels or even the right towels or having our fridges restocked in a timely manner.As for where you ate, we were a bit confused when we first got there as no one explained to us where we could eat. I finally asked some other Americans if we paid for the pizzas since we saw the 12 dollar price by them. They were nice enough to let us know to ignore the prices and that all was free. We ate at the Buffet in the Caribe since we knew for sure that was included. Didn't know if we could eat at the Beach Buffet or not. The food at the Caribe was decent that night. Lots of seafood stuff for those of you who like seafood there was plenty to be had. Had the pasta bar and found some fries on the buffet line. Later on in the week found they could cook up fresh steak, pork chops, grouper and a few other seafood type things. The breakfast buffet at the Caribe was smaller than the Beach Buffet. At the Beach Buffet, you could have the chef cook up some fresh bacon for you while you wait for your omelet. A few times people in my group got some spoiled pineapple but they knew right away and stopped eating it. Otherwise, there are a lot of things to eat for breakfast. My sisters had hard boiled eggs, oatmeal, fried eggs, plenty of fruit, donuts, banana cake/muffins and lots of other things. Ate at the buffet for lunch and had some wonderful soups and had the usual pasta bar or had fried chicken. Or had them cook up a few pork chops for me. Then for dinner, we found the Golf resort buffet and their chef there seasoned the pork chops wonderfully, wished I had found him earlier in the week and would have eaten there. The Beach Buffet guys were good but all they put on was a little salt as opposed to the Golf buffet chef, the chops were excellent and juicy and perfectly done. They also had calamari, veal, steak, pork chops, oysters, grouper and another type of fish cook to order. They also had the best desserts or we got lucky that night where everything I had like the chocolate brownie cake was awesome as well as the white cake with a boysenberry middle was moist and to die for. We did eat at the Mexican restaurant and as others have said the portions are small but their salad bar has tacos and ready to make and fill quesadillas. The steak place we ate for lunch and that was decent, the steak was a done well even though we asked for medium but it was tasty nonethe less. The Italian place was good too, I think I had breaded chop but after reading someone else's review it could have been veal with a egg on top. Tried to go to the seafood restaurant but the hours were only from noon to 5 p.m.Out of the 9 of us, 4 of us got a bit of the Montezuma's revenge but not the full blown version that keeps you in the room for days. A few of them had salad but not sure if that was the real culprit. So, beware. The drinks were plentiful and always had more than enough rum in them. Their regular fruit drinks were pretty tasty too.My sister got a massage for an hour which cost 45 bucks and she said it was pretty good. The beach was nice and walked to the market area for souvenier buying. They weren't really into bartering as good as some other places we've been but were able to pay a better price then was originally being asked. We went on the trip to Isla Soana. Don't believe that Michael Jackson got married in the church at Chavon because he didn't. I think they use that as a hook to get you to go on the Alto de Chavon trip. It's also a replica and not a real village. Saw the Chavon river where they made Anaconda. Then took the speed boat to the natural pool in the Caribbean Sea and that was awesome to get out in the middle of the Sea and be in an area that simply looks like a pool in the middle of nowhere. Then went on to Soana where the beach was great and the water pretty shallow so no one was in jeopardy of drowning. The water was nice the further you went out. That day was so hot that our catamaran ride back was excruciatingly painful. We were hot and sunburned and there was not a breeze to be had. That was one of the longest times of the whole trip. If they tell you that you will get to shop, you won't be able to do much shopping in different shops. We stop at a place that has a bathroom and sells stuff and that's pretty much your shopping trip. Better off walking down the beach for that. I was a bit disappointed with the trip because of what I read previous to my trip it made it sound awesome. Just another day at the beach just somewhere else in DR instead of at the resort. Anyway, if you have any questions please let me know. I will probably not go back to another big resort. We've been to smaller resorts the past 4 years and we were all pretty happy with the way we were treated at the smaller places. After going to the more personal places this place made us feel like a herd of sheep that no one cared to get to know or want to know. The people are nice but they just didn't give us the warm and fuzzy feelings that we got in Puerto Plata, Runaway Bay, Costa Rica, and Cancun. But that is just my preference.Overall, this vacation was good not great. There were just things here and there that I noticed that was different from all my other experiences. If you like being surrounded by lots of people then this is the place for you. I much prefer the more intimate and smaller resorts.

<Author>smorrow66
<Content>Beach is Greatness! Just came back on June 1, 2006 after 4 night stay. I will give it an overall three and break it down. First, the bad: The food was about a 2 out of 5. It just wasnt very good, but there was plenty of it. The Steakhouse had one of the toughest pieces of meat I have eaten in awhile. The okay/good: The service - I thought the staff was very friendly, but they were reserved. Language is a minor issue, because the overwhelming number of guests were other Spanish speakers, many from Espana itself, but alot from Central and South America. The other large group was the Dutch. The number of Americans and Canadians was small, but all the staff knew enough English that communication wasnt really an issue. Remember people, you arent in America, you are in the Republica Dominicana and it wouldnt hurt anyone to learn three very important Spanish words: Por Favor and Da Nada and Gracias. The very best feature was the beach. White soft sand amid beautiful palm trees and the Bavaro beach is virturally wave free because of the sandbar offshore that breaks the surf well out to sea. The snorkling off the beach at the reef was greatness. My daughter is 10 and too young to dive but I didnt feel that I missed out because the water is not more than 25 to 30 feet deep at the reef and we easily dove down on it without tanks. If you go, dont go for the food, politely ask them to switch to English - Habla Ingles Por Favor? and just enjoy that beautiful beach.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Wasn't what we expected, but gorgeous! My firend and I (2 girls) 27 and 26, were psyched to party in Punta Cana since February 06 when we booked this trip. We went from 5/25 - 5/30. We spoke to our travel agent who informed us that there weren't alot of kids at this resort. Granted, she was right, but there were alot of couples and some families. We were expecting more single people, so if your looking for Hedonism, this isn't it. HOWEVER, I agree with the other posts, vacation IS what you make of it, so we had a good time, regardless. There is plenty of food to choose from...the cafe con leche is the best! They have bottled water everywhere, but we still managed to get sick from day 2 on. Watch out, don't forget, like we did, that those yummy pina coladas are made with ice. The liquor selection was crap! If you like your grey goose, jack and so on, you better bring it with you, duty free....we had a layover in P.R....absolute was 10 bucks! OH YEAH! This was the best, when we did get sick and went to the shop for immodium (forgot it in another bag at home..DOH!), 5 bucks... PER PILL! We didn't even bother buying it. Pack it, don't forget it! What else, oh we wnet horseback riding for an hour for twenty bucks! We asked the guys selling packages in the front. They pick u up at the casino, and take u to the ranch. If you've never been before, its a cool, but painful experience. Oh and no lessons, u just get on and go, the guide follows you. I would definitely get the massage on the beach after the horse riding, like we did for 25 bucks, it was heaven! Especially since the beds are hard! lol! The rooms were nice, not 5 star quality or anything, but what u would expect in the caribbean. We had a balcony, the air conditioner was actually too cold at night, and the hot water was always hot. Our room was cleaned evry day ...that we remembered to put the sign on the door. The disco was fun, we had a great time there, and its only a short walk, or if you happen to catch the trolley, in front of the Caribe, even better. Overall it was a fun trip, I just wished that we booked it with more of our friends.

<Author>SumiVancouver_BC
<Content>So-So I stayed at the Barcelo Bavaro Caribe from April 22 -28. This was my second time to Punta Cana and first time to this resort. This resort looked quite beautiful from its appearances. We had to wait 3 hours to be checked in but that was to be expected. Our room on the fourth floor with the view of the gardens and had all the basic amenities. On the first three days, our toilet broke twice and the AC broke once. The fourth day was problem free but not for long. The fifth and sixth day, the lights were working in the room. The good news was that they maintenance staff were in our room fixing the problems within five minutes of our phone call. I was very impressed by their punctuality. There weren any lights in the sleeping area therefore it was pretty dark at the night. The rooms were cleaned very well everyday and the mini fridge was filled everyday. The buffet wasn too impressing or great at all. There wasn that much selection of items to choose from. We loved the Mexican restaurant where we ate dinner three times and Italian restaurant was pretty good as well for both lunch and dinner. The nice thing about the resort was that we didn have to make reservation for the restaurants as they were all first come first serve basis.The nightly shows at the resort were pretty entertaining. We went the Tropicalisimio and were bored to death and left half way through. I noticed that there were other people leaving as well in the middle of the show. The discos were pretty good except that it was spring break time for Spain and the place was filled up with teens. Mind you that we were only in our early 20. It was too much of loud kids to handle. We took a two hour horse back riding tour at the resort for $40 each from 4 -6 pm. We enjoyed it a lot except we were extremely sore for couple of days after that. My friend got some skin tear in an area we won discuss. This excursion is not meant for kids and make sure that you are dressed well. A second excursion we did was Altos de Chavon and exploration of the cave. This excursion was breathtaking and quite interesting. Sting had performed at Altos de Chavon the night before and we got to see the big mess of garbage that was left behind after the show. It was quite an experience.  Overall, the staffs at the resort were awesome and very helpful. There were barely any lineups for drinks. The beaches were gorgeous and the water was the perfect temperature. I wouldn personally return to this resort again but will recommend it for the teenagers. And watch out for mosquitoes. We took mosquito repellent and it didn do a darn thing.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Foreign, tropical, a nice getaway! I went to Barcelo Bavaro Garden in 2002 with my parents and boyfriend. My room consisted of 2 separate beds, and my parents' queen was composed of 2 smaller beds pushed together..as I have seen other places I'm sure. Every day we were entitled to breakfast, lunch and dinner. You could choose to eat between the beach and garden's restaurants. The food was not memorable to me, buffet had a lot of unfamiliar dishes so I stuck to ones I knew, which were not anything special. One thing that was amazing was the fruit! VERY YUMMY!!! Lots of it, fresh, and juicy, especially the pineapple. At lunch, you can get thin personal pizzas made in front of you, lineups can be long so you come back in a while, but they are yummy. The pool was nice, ocean was beautiful. Everything was clean. Here and there people will take pictures of you and ask you for money for them (bigger than normal size, and clear, but pricey) Kayaks, canoes, etc. to entertain you. Entertainment every night featuring dances or audience oriented games. A little shop on site to buy convenience foods, but very expensive. Staff are always getting people to dance and play games! Very nice staff. You can go on excursions during the day ie. horseback riding (poor skinny horses), the zoo, cuban cigar making tour where you go see the village and local schools (where you can purchase items to give to students yourself) safari tour. If you are concerned about your children seeing nudity, don't bring them here. This place isnt a over the top high class, but its no dump!!Very ordinary, but fun! Go here if you want to have fun, do your own thing, and you're not depending on high class food or events. Don't drink the water! Have fun!! It's what you make of it!

<Content>This place is so-so My family and I just returned from Punta Cana early this morning. We stayed at the Caribe. I had high expectations. Don't get me wrong, it was very pretty and the food was good, but the people were not very friendly at all. Two years ago we stayed at Sunscape (now Punta Cana Grand) and when we left, we felt as if we were leaving family. We did not feel that at all this time. The service was just average. It seemed as if the workers hardly ever smiled. It was sad. I know they work hard, and long hours, but how they treat the tourists makes a big difference on how you feel about the place. They were not overly friendly at all. And the evening shows were pretty bad. I do realize that they do these shows over and over again, and for them it may get old, but they should realize that for those who are only there for a week or so, they do not want to feel as if we are putting the performers out by having to put on a show. I know it's hard when you have somewhere else to compare it to, but I really wouldn't recommend this resort to anyone. The rooms smelled very musty and it felt dingy. My husband and son ended up with several bug bites during the nights (in the room.) The beach was very nice though. There was a bit more topless sunbathers than I would have liked, but I can deal with that, and it seemed like soooo many people smoked. I felt as if I was constantly breathing in second hand smoke. My children however had a wonderful time. It really was nice, I am just comparing it to Sunscape, and I realize that may not be fair, but I would rather go there again than to Barcelo.

<Content>Beautiful-Great time Place is beautiful, travel agents HORRIBLE. FUNJET TOTALLY SCREWED US!!! When I booked this vacation it was for 4 adults all inclusive at a price per adult. When I recieved my itenerary everything looked good, no problems. When I got here, they put all four adults in ONE TINY ROOM! We were stuck for a whole week all together (One couple mind you..romantic huh). I had to call on my cell to FUNJET and took 20 minutes to get through on international Roam. I can only imagine how much my cell bill will cost. With them basically saying...too bad. Now I am in the process of fighting the charges. No where on my iten did it say we had 1 room. As a matter of fact, if you try and book directly from this hotel, they wont even ALLOW you to put four adults in one room. All funjet had to say was 'one reservation one room'. I said so if I would have booked 6 people on one reservation, you would have put all of us in one room? He was like um no. No mistake on my part my reservation clearly said FOUR ADULTS, so there was no confusion that this was like 2 adults and two kids. I figured that they would accomodate 4 adults appropriately. WRONG!! So they basically made out on us. The hotel was completely booked so they could not accomodate us. They did however, evenually upgrade our room to the beach side, but the room was still the same size, if not smaller.Now onto the Good:Don't believe the bad reviews posted here about this place. I would say consider the source (where they are writing from) before you believe any bad stories about this place. I have traveled a lot of places and the beaches here are the most gorgeous I have ever seen. The sand has a hint of pink in it from the coral. I am a diver and there was a lot of species of coral that I have never seen before, however, the marine life was not in abundance. The food is good, but not the greatest. Always go for the buffets, they are your best bet. Always tip the maid staff and they will stock your fridge with beer. A lot of people do not speak English here. It is their country, they speak their language. Make an effort to try and speak their language. Important words: beer = cervasa, bathroom = bano, ola = hello, please = por favor, thank you = gracious... those are the basics. The grounds here are beautiful, the people are very nice. Rooms are very clean. It had a better than expected staffed work out facility (considering it is a 3rd world country). It is very safe here and we walked all the way up the beach for an hour and a half. Try and eat at a cafe off the beaten path if you can. They have a market here and if you go, definately barter. They will start out ridicously high for items. I would definately stay here again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great Scenery......stay at Beach or Palace not Caribe Can't beat the beach and I have been fortunate enough to have been to many. This is three beach front resorts Caribe, Beach, Palace side by side with side walk connections. There is also two that are not beach front but are connected, Casino Hotel and Golf Hotel. The Beach and Palace should meet most Americans expectations while the Caribe will fall short. The grounds to both are roughly the same but the service and food are definately better at Beach and Palace. You have access to all resorts and amenities equally except the food at the Palace is at a premium. I went with a group of six and experienced no check-in problems that has been written about here but we arrived around 3pm and there was no crowd. Main disapointment was that the hobie cats cost 25-35 dollars an hour, all other all-inclusive resorts I have visted included without charge. If you go looking for pampering this may fall short but if you go looking for a safe relaxing vacation with a beatiful setting you will pobably succeed. I would gladly go back but am not sure my wife would.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>a holiday to remember My daughter and I just returned from our holiday to the Dominican Republic. We thoroughly enjoyed our stay. We really wanted a nice relaxing place by the water, and that's exactly what we got. The beach is amazing. The sand is like brown sugar. The pools were kept very clean, even though it was very windy and sand kept blowing in it. Our room was clean, and the beds were comfortable. The showers were clean, hot, lots of pressure. The rooms have a safe, and a stocked fridge of pop, beer, and water. Our patio faced a courtyard, very relaxing, we could also see the ocean from it. Resort has a train that takes you around the property to the different hotels. Played Mini-golf several times, night and day. Never played at the golf course, although heard form other guests that it was pretty good. Took in the nightly entertainment, it was quite funny. They get the audience involved. There big show Tropicallissimo was nice too, but we enjoyed the nightly shows better. I found the service to be good, I wish we spoke Spanish though, that would help with the language barrier. You always get better service with a smile, please and thank-you. Tipping is not required, but most people do it when they receive god service. Try to get off the resort and see the Dominican. We loved our excursions, Bavaro Trackers, Bavaro Runners, and a day trip to Isla Saona. The Dominican is breathtaking. You also see the way they really live, the people are very attractive, music is a very big part of their life. Would certainly go back.

<Author>timman19
<Content>We Loved This Place! This is a very nice all-inclusive resort located around a 20 minute drive from the airport.This is great resort if you looking to spend some time at the beach and by the pool.There are several parts to this resort and this was the first one built. You have access to the pools and beaches at the other resorts as well as the casino and disco. There is a trolley that runs every 15 minutes that makes stops at every other hotel.Our room needed a bit of work but was fine. It was clean and there were no strange smells of any kind. The bathroom size was fine but the toilet is located in a separate room which is very handy if one person is using the shower or the sink.This resort has double and single rooms. There are no king or queen sized beds to be found. We had double that had two double beds which they had pushed together since it was the two of us.The refrigerator is stocked each day with beer and sodas at no charge. There was also coffee provided as well. Each room has a balcony which is a nice size and good to sit out in and enjoy the weather.The only bad part about the rooms was the lack of drawer space. We pretty much had to leave our clothes in our luggage. There is also not a whole lot a room for your luggage in the closet. We barely fit two bags in there. There is also a safe for your use and you can choose the combination yourself.The service at check in was excellent. All of the front desk clerks speak English quite well. A porter will take you to your room which I recommend as it is hard to find the room by yourself. Our porter did not speak much English but was very nice.The food here was very good. At this hotel there is a buffet and an Italian restaurant. The buffet has three meals a day and the Italian place is a sit down that also has a pizza place next door that serves pretty good mini pies from noon until midnight. These two places are included in the package.Nearby, is a steakhouse, Mexican restaurant and another buffet. These are at the Beach hotel which is a short walk away. All but the buffet are sit down. There is a line sometimes for some of the restaurants but the food was very good.The buffets are your only choice for breakfast. They have made to order eggs and omletes as well as a buffet where you can help yourself. The service in all of the restaurants and buffets was excellent. They are very attentive but not all of them speak English but most understand enough to get by.The beach is wonderful and it one of the best in the Caribbean. There are plenty of lounge charis but get their early to get a good spot. The beach is topless which may come as a surprise to may Americans visiting.The pool is also great. It round and features an island in the middle. The deeper parts of the pool are wider for swimming while the shallow parts tend to be narrow which is great for the kids. Both the beach and the pool were very clean and well maintained.The pool fills up early. There is an honor system whereby people place their towels on chairs to hold them. Even early in the morning, seats have been reserved. Your best bet is to grab one early, eat breakfast and then go back.Towels are available for the pool and the beach. They give you a card for each person which is returned to you when you bring the towels back. They didn give us these at check in so ask for them then. I went back but didn have a problem.The all-inclusive package is also good at any bar on the resort. They have an all-inclusive drink menu that is quite large and has a wide selection. Our hotel featured nightly entertainment which was music of some sort of comedy show. They were good and entertaining but didn start until 10:00 p.m.The casino is a bit small but never closes. I didn go in the disco but it appeared to be very popular based on the line to get in one night. There are few places to shop but not too much to choose from. We didn buy anything as far as souvineers go.Do not drink the tap water! Drink bottled water only. If you make coffee in your room, use the bottled water that they provide. You will probably get sick if you drink from the tap.Also bring mosquito repellant. They can be a pain at night. The store in the lobby has it for sale but it was $15 for a small bottle. We decided to pass on that price.There is also plenty of security here. You will be given a wristband that identifies where you are staying that you should never remove. The security was pleasant and their job is to make sure that everyone there is supposed to be there. They were armed with big nightsticks and at night they tend to stay in the dark and keep an eye on things. You are completely safe there as there were plenty of guards.I recommend arranging for a transfer from the airport to the hotel. Taxi drivers have to be negotiated with but transfers are much more reliable. Also, stick to the resort. You can walk up the beach but you will be warned when to go no further. The Dominican Republic is a poor nation and tourists tend to stick out and can be targeted. There is plenty to do here anyway. There are also some trips you can take and those are escorted and can be arranged through representatives in the lobby.Again, the service here was excellent. They really try to make you happy. It helps if you speak Spanish. My wife does and I think we got a bit more attention from them because of that. If you are coming from the United States, bring a bunch of singles and small bills for tips. Tipping is not required but if you have a good server, a few American dollars is nice. They love that due to the rate of exchange and theyl remember you when you go back.Ie been to a few islands in the Caribbean and the majority of the tourists there were Americans. Not here. Most are from Europe (France, Germany, Italy and Spain), and a large number of Canadians. Americans were the minority but there were many of them around. It interesting to meet people from other parts of the world and most people that we met were very nice.Overall, we enjoyed ourselves very much and will be returning there again.  
<Date>Jan 24, 2006

<Author>Chipielolo
<Content>Hated this hotel We just came back from a stay at the Barcelo Bavaro Caribe Hotel. We were there for 8 days, and we didn't have a good stay. The worst part was the attittude of the staff: for a handful (4 to 5 people top) of smiling employees, the majority was really rude and acted like if we were bothering them, or worse, not even present. For example, one of the staff member came and took the ping pong paddles from my husband and son's hands without a word of explanation, 1/2 h before the activities stopped and left without a word or an excuse... we thought that lady was kidding and stayed speechless as she answered to our question very seriously and without a look back: closed. The staff at the front counter is rude (slapping the counter to call the next on line without a word)and unhelpful: my sister had a courtesy room (after refusing to pay the $25 they asked for) for 10mn not one more or we'll charge you whith dirty towels, no hand soap and dirty open beds. They were asked to leave their luggage in front of their old room from noon to 7 PM without supervision.The beach staff refused to lend my brother in law a windsurf at 3:30 (the rental finished at 5, but he told him he wouldn't be back by 4, the time in his book he was to refuse to begin to rent.) The only nice employees we had were the pool towels ones. They actually said HI, and we even saw a smile...The rooms were old and very humid: the mirrors were permanently full of steam, and the floor wet. The air conditionning was freezing and very noisy. If the cleaning lady put it on after doing our room, we were doomed to enter a freezer... my sister found a coakroach in her bathroom, we had one dropped on our table at the restaurant. We had no hot water 3 out of the 8 days.We gave tips every meal we had, and left money on our pellow every morning, it didn't make any difference. We thought we might get a second washcloth, but no, it was the same one for the whole week, washed and put to dry in the shower...Our toilet made a terrible noise, we had to actually cut the water off every night.When you called to have something fixed, they would ask what room, listen to what was broke, say thank you... and that was the end of it...The food was horrible, always the same thing, it smell like airplane food. I got sick twice, and I was very careful of what I ate. The bread tasted like plaster, the coffee like caramel, the fruit were hit or miss (it could be one sweet slice of pineapple after 4 sour). Same with the meat: In the same restaurant 2 days in a row, I had for the same item on the menu, 2 different cut of meat, one OK, and the other one with a very strong flavor ( I ate only one piece and almost spit it out).The only OK restaurant (in which that happened matter of factly) was a grill on the beach, but IF we got a table after 2 hours wait and our name on the booking paper, the waitresses were rude and you didn't have twice in a row the same thing. We asked for grilled shrimp and got 3 on a plate with cold french fries and old lettuce. we asked for a second plate and it was mount of shrimp and no french fries.One good part was a pizza place open for take out, so when we didn't eat anything we could order a pizza ( very small) and eat on the beach... there again, you could get lucky or not: they were using either mozarella or a very gross and strong white cheese... nobody could eat it.I was counting the days before we had to go home and the dinners/lunchs we had left to suffer. Towards the end, I would eat bananas only and try my luck on pizza.There is plenty of resorts on the Dominican Republic island, do not waste your time or take a chance at this hotel. I know I won't!

<Content>Very enjoyable, be relaxed, be patient This review is coming from an english speaking Canadian who was travelling with his beautiful french speaking girlfriend. We completely and totally enjoyed this hotel and resort. The access to all of the other resorts was perfect. The food was not excellent, but there were places where the food was just amazing, The Steakhouse for example was by far the best restaurant. The service was not fast by any means, but you are on vacation, relax and go with the flow and you will have a blast. A lot of the staff did not speak english, but there were some who did. All of the staff were nice, and if they were not we ignored them, again, you are on a holiday, who cares about their bad moods! The spanish language barrier was a challenge, but when all you want is water or booze from a waitress or bartender it is very easy, and there are a large number of english speaking staff that will be more than happy to help you in any way that they can.We found all of the staff very nice, both english and non english speaking. They were all doing anything and everything that they could to help us to enjoy our stay. Best Vacation to date for us, a great choice for rest and relaxation, great beach/weather/pool. Ask for extra cleanliness in your room and you will get it.

<Content>Barcelo Not So Bad We traveled Thanksgiving week. There was 11 of us. The ages ranged from 9 to 62. I was scared of what we were getting into after reading the reviews for the last 5 months. I also left $1 in the refg. for the person filling the refg. with drinks, we got extra beer and coke. The food was OK, the buffet had mostly Dom. Rep. food. The beaches were the best thing there. They were BEAUTIFUL!!! There was topless sun bathing at the beach and pool. My nieces are 9  11. We warned them there would by topless on the beach. Not many people speak english. We did not have any problems. All of the shows were in Spanish. But I told my family what do you except we were in a spanish speaking country. (Jamaica had us spoiled because most everyone spoke english.) The day you leave make sure that your departure time from the hotel is at least 3 hours before your flight. We left 2 1/4 hours before and by the time we got to our gate we had enough time to go to the restroom. We seemed rushed. All and All our vacation was GOOD.

We hardly ever went to the pool, was very windy and water was cold. <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Ended up at the Barcelo Bavaro on Accident, but Enjoyed It! I went on this vacation as a last minute special with 3 other twentysomething females and we had a great time. Everything is what you make of it so I believe all of the negative reviews must have had way too high expectations and need completely catered to in order to have a good time. We were supposed to be at the IFS Villas Bavaro, but due to their air conditioning being out, we were transferred to the Barcelo Bavaro Caribe instead. We had no problems at check in. We spoke some very poor Spanish, but the front desk was very helpful, even in English. We were given two rooms next to each other. When one of the rooms had a leaky faucet, they were transferred to a beach front room. The rooms are average but the AC worked fine. The cleaning ladies could be a little slow some days and forgot to leave us towels two different days, but we called the front desk and towels were delivered in 10 minutes.The weather was fabulous everyday. There may have been 10 minutes of rain, but it was then gorgeous. The activity staff always tried to keep you busy at the pool and beach (beware of many Europeans wearing speedos or being topless around the water) with water aerobics, frisbee rum (win and keep the bottle), dance lessons, etc. You did have to get to the pool pretty early on some days to get chairs, but if they were taken, we just drug up chairs from the beach with no problem. The staff also ran the evening entertainment - some shows were okay, the Talent Show was horrible.We were always waited on quickly at the pool bar (maybe there are some advantages to being younger blonde females). We did have to sometimes wait longer when there were female bartenders, but I've received worse service from female bartenders in the US.The food was fine. For those complaining that the Barcelo food made you ill, you must not have been to the Dominican before. It's not just this hotel, it's most of them (we've been twice and met others who had been 4 times to 4 different hotels and were ill each time). The food is different and your body will react to it. Take 2 Pepto Bismo tablets before each meal and it's not that bad. You may have some bowel issues after eating, but it's not something that's going to keep you in your bathroom for the night. We were at the discoteque and casino having a fabulous time each night. The Mexican restaurant and steakhouse were excellent and we never waited more than 10 minutes. The buffets are okay, but the pasta bar was always very good (and doesn't make you sick).This hotel was good for relaxing and enjoying the sunshine. It had a nice atmosphere and with the right attitude, you can have a very good time. I'll admit that I've been to some extremely nice 5* or better resorts in the past year in Hawaii and the US Virgin Islands and it does not compare to that. We knew that going in. Make sure your expectations are realistic, relax, and have a good time!  
<Date>Nov 21, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Fantastic My husband and I stayed at the Caribe from June 15-21. We had an excellent time! The beach and resort are both beautiful! The rooms were nicer than I expected, clean, but did seem to have an overall dampness to them, but what do you expect when it is like 100 degrees outside with 100% humidity! The staff seemed ok, my husband speaks fluent spanish so that helped, but when some people write that the staff was rude, I find that hard to believe. I don't speak hardly any spanish at all and got along just fine. If they couldn't understand me they would just kind of smile. What's wrong with a smile?! Don't get me wrong, this is not a resort where they wait on you hand and foot, but it was great all the same. The food did get monotonous after a while at the buffet, but we visited some of the restaurants, and they were great! The only real dissapointment was that it was soooo hot, it was very hard to enjoy dinner when sweat is running down your face! Also, I would have liked to have had somewhere on the beach to get drinks, we had to keep going back to the pool bar every 20 minutes. But we needed the exercise! Definately take your own medicine and sunscreen, and use it! My husband is dark to begin with, but the sun down there is so strong that even he got burned! The place is not perfect, but considereing you are in an underdeveloped country where most of the population are poor, you are treated like a king compared to them. Be nice and smile and they will be nice back! For the people who complained, you should be ashamed of yourself! Problems happen in the nicest hotels, unfortunately DR is less equipped to deal with them! Go there, have a good time and enjoy yourselves, we did!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Loved It!!! I recently just returned from Barcelo Bavaro Caribe Hotel and had an awesome time!!!! The resort is breath taking! the beach is pure white sand and beautiful blue waters. My Boyfriend and I would spend the whole day relaxing by the beach.The weather was great also. Before my trip i read online that the weather was going to be terrible that is was going to rain everyday, but the weather was beautiful and hot everyday. If you want to get a tan this is def the place to go. The Food was pretty good but at the buffets its just the same thing everyday so you get sick of it. Meats, Potatoes, Pastas, Fish, Salads, and breads. My Favorite at the Buffets was the pasta salad. The Mexican was our favorite but let me tell you the service is terrible. First of all we waited online for 1 hour and then were ignored by all the workers and waited about 20 mintutes for a glass of water. The steakhouse was very good the sirlion was the best and my boyfriend liked the bbq pork ribs so try it out!The Italian was ok and the pizza def didnt taste the same, also terrible service. Drinks were pretty good but always hard to get. The bar by the pool was always crowded and once again the service was terrible it would take forever to get one drink. Def try the bahama mama drink very tasty!!:) Also i would def recommend going on the Saona Island Excursion it was the best. Its an all day excursion visiting a natural pool in the middle of the ocean and visiting a beautiful beach. On the way there you take a very fast speed boat and on the way back a catameran. They have music and drinks so its a lot of fun. Be careful with the Domincan Rum my boyfriend got very sick from it. We had such a great time and def def would go back. Some more helpful tips bring sunblock, medicines, and even snacks from home because everything is soooo expensive. Sunblock was 36 dollars a lighter was 10 dollars and chips were 10 dollars. Absolutely crazy!. Please email me with any questions!!!

<Content>Terrible Place to stay My family and I are from Miami, FL plus another couple went to Barcelo Bavaro Caribe, and stayed there in 2004 in the month of July for a 7 day all inclusive vacation package. We were a bit skeptical about the reviews we had read, but, nevertheless, we went with a good attitude. From the time we arrived these are the problems we experienced.1. There was a couple that were honeymooners, and wanted to change rooms since their sheets were bloody!! Management said they had to wait until the following morning.2. The rooms are a bit lower class looking, and the dresser had no drawers just two bifold doors with shelves. The only hotel in that chain that the dressers have drawers is the Barcelo Bavaro Palace.3. The pool had broken tiles all around the borders, and inside the pool. My 7 year old daughter cut her foot because of this.4. Every day we had problems with the towels. We would not get enough, and one day by the end of the day the room had not been serviced, and we had no towels, and had to wait about 45 minutes for them.5. Around the third day things got really bad. Our bathroom toilet overflooded in the middle of the night, Water was coming down the balcony. the following day we spent almost the entire morning complaining with management about this issue, and getting it resolved. They gave us another room at the Bavaro Beach, and that toilet had problems as well.6. One day at the lobby while we were resolving some other issues, and my daughter approached one of the hotel employees about some paintings they were selling, just being curious, and she mentioned she was thirsty, and the employee sent my daughter without our permission all the way to the bar area..to get something to drink. All of a sudden I could not find my daughter, and 15 minutes passed until the employee approached, and told me she had sent my daughter to the bar area for a drink of water since she was thirsty.7. The couple we were with got really sick with vomiting and diarreah. As a result of this we had to cancel a tour to an island which we did 24 hours in advance. M.K. tours Representatives procrastinated until the end of our vacation to give us our money back. It was at the airport that my friend and I approached a general manager of M.K. tours. Told him the story, about the tour, and how his employees were planning to rip us off our money. This resulted in a major complaint with the tour agency M.K. Tours located in Coral Gables, Fl when we arrived in town. After a drawn out letter to the agency, and them giving us the run around, we received from the owner of the agency a 1 week hotel voucher to THE SAME PLACE. Needless, to say we are definately not going back to that same resort. This year we are going to Ocean Blue which is a newer resort so I will give you my input when I get back since I am leaving on 6/25. If I had anything positive to say about Punta Cana is the beach is really nice, and the food is good. That's about it.

<Author>ajvald
<Content>Nice and Relaxing Vacation We just returned from our trip to Bavaro Beach Resort in Punta Cana. We stayed at the Bavaro Caribe Hotel, but had wristbands for all-hotel access (our tour guide arranged it for an additional fee). I had some initial hesitations about going to Punta Cana (this was my first time) after reading a lot of the negative reviews. However, I must say that we (my husband and in-laws) had an absolutely wonderful time! We arrived at the resort on Friday and immediately began enjoying the activities and facilities. Here was our overall experience:1. Transportation- Definately a lot easier when it is pre-arranged! Taxis are also readily available, but were a lot more expensive.2. Hotel Room- Not as modern as some of the better 5-star hotels, but they kept them very neat and clean. We also had a beautiful view of the beach.They kept the mini bar stocked with H2O, beer and soda.3. Hotel Grounds- Landscaping was beautiful and clean. The cleaning staff was hard at work early in the morning every day. 4. Food- The restaurants were mostly good. Service was pretty good, but it is a lot easier if you speak Spanish (which we did). We encountered an occasional non-friendly staff member, but you find one of those anywhere you go. Buffets were usually the best for breakfast; lunch and dinner tasted the same to me! The best restuarants in my opinion were Las Brisas and El Rincon Dominicano (both on Bavaro Palace grounds). We had excellent Lobster in Las Brisas and fantastic Dominican food in El Rincon. Drinks were always good (try the coco loco)! Be prepared to gain some weight if you don't plan on being active.5. Entertainment- Day entertainment was good (mostly activities with the hotel guests) poolside and night entertainment involved a lot of singing and dancing. We didn't really enjoy Tropicalissimo, but we liked the Caribe Hotel entertainment a lot! 6. Tipping/Money/Souvenirs- Bring lots of singles for tipping! Change was hard to get and tipping improved level of service dramatically. Bring your own suntan oil, medicine and other necessities. The suntan oil at the hotel cost $30 US dollars! Souvenir shopping was mediocore at best and involves a lot of haggling at the market on the beach. We avoided it.Overall, we had a great time. Keep in mind that if you don't speak Spanish, it is somewhat more difficult to participate in many of the activities. The staff do not all speak Spanish, but they always try their best to accomodate non-Spanish speakers. A lot of the activities were primarly spoken in spanish, but if that's something you don't mind, then you will enjoy it. After all, you are vacationing in the Dominican Republic!  
<Date>Jun 9, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Fantastic My husband and I stayed at the Barcelo Bavaro-Caribe for our honeymoon from May 24th to May 30th. Had I known I would love it that much I would have stayed longer. It was amazing. The weather was perfect and the hospitality we received was fantastic. We were even given a beautiful flower arrangement and complimentary bottle of champagne because we were newlyweds. My only complaint was that we didn't have one king size bed, rather it was two queen beds pushed together. I also think the hotels should carry calling cards as well. It seemed that the only place on the resort that carried calling cards was the music shop in La Plaza Dominicana, and that store was closed at times. My suggestion would be to buy your calling card prior to arriving on the island. To follow up on some posts about the food, please keep in mind the fact that they are catering to different ethinicities and can't use too many spices therefore it may be bland to some but perfectly delicious to others. Every one has different tastes so that has to be taken into consideration. The food was decent and edible enough and there were some things that were out right delicious. You need to be the judge of it without being influenced by others. The staff was welcoming and accomodating. The only other drawback I found was that there was no real souvenir shopping. The resorts have a lock on the gift shops and the prices were a bit outrageous. One shop had the nerve to quote me $11 US dollars for a refridgerator magnet. I nearly collapsed from laughing so hard. They don't fill up to much so you will have the shop owners cornering you into coming into their shops to buy. Just be prepared to hear some outrageous prices and be prepared to try to haggle as best you can. My husband did and it worked well in one shop, not so well in another. But the shops are owned independently, not by the hotels so they are not to blame in this regard as well. All in all I have nothing but praise for the hotel resort. The fact that you can go and eat and drink in any of the other hotels was also a huge PLUS (except for the Palace. That was the only hotel not all-inclusive to the guests of the other 4 hotels.) If you are staying at the Palace then you can eat and drink at all 5 hotels. I can't wait to go back! FYI: Bring mosquito repellent. My husband and I were ravished by the mosquitos (the island having come off of a 10 day rain period prior to our arrival). The mosquitos come out at night, but that obviously, is not the fault of the hotel.

<Author>Jeansnow
<Content>Two Weeks is Too Long We stayed at the Barcelo Bavaro Caribe' Resort from April 25th to May 9th 2005.I can't say enough about the beautiful grounds, they are kept very manicured, by so many hard working people.The beach is fantastic too, with white powdery sand and crystal clear turquoise water.Overall it wasn't a bad resort, although we had some minor problems.Two weeks is really too long though.I didn't find the people there overly friendly, even though we tipped generously, and gave lots of gifts too. At the Mexican restaurant we were left sitting for a half hour after we had been given menus, after that length of time we just left. I don't know if they were ignoring us, or they had forgotten us. We had been there the night before and had great service, and the workers had been very friendly. At our own buffett we found the people to be quite friendly, of course there again, we tipped them at every meal and gave every one of them gifts too.The food wasn't what we were used to, it is their local food, and I have to say our standards for cleanliness are much higher. However the selection was very good, and we certainaly never went hungry. The reception people were very matter of fact too, with hardly a smile.Thank God for Nancy!!, our tour director (Signature)She had answers to all of our questions (and we had a lot of questions)I broke a tooth off my partial plate while I was there and she even got me some crazy glue to hold it in place until I got home to a dentist.We went to the entertainment at all of the resorts as well as the Tropicalissimo Show, which was fantastic!The casino was fun. The train rides were great too.I don't think that any of the bartenders gave me spirits in my drinks (even once), that I didn't have to ask for it :-( and I only had 5 drinks the whole time I was there, and my husband doesn't drink at all.We took gifts for the Outback Safari to distribute to the villagers  schools that they support, I think they do a wonderful service!We thought the trip itself would be a little too rigorous for us at our age.So, to sum it all up.........I would go to the same resort again, but just for the beautiful grounds ,the beach,  the walking in the park behind the convention center which we did every day, to enjoy the birds and flowers there.Please people, we pay a lot for our vacations there and we know that you work very hard for a very little bit of money, that is why we tip so generously and come bearing gifts for you. A smile is the only thanks we require. We love the Dominican and plan to return at Christmastime.

The only bar we could find that was close to fair service was the lobby/pool bar at the Golf. <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Had an awesome time!! :) I just got back from staying at the Barcelo Bavaro Beach Resort. I'm 16 years old and i had the best time! Theres plenty to do, so you never get bored! Some of the activities there are kayaking, and snorkeling. There is also streching,aerobics, volleyball, and dance lessons every morning! Your trip is what you make of it, so get involved! The food was nothing to brag about. However, you are in another country so keep that in mind. You should be careful of what you eat but don't be so worried about it! The hotel grounds are beautiful, that goes for the whole resort. There are security gaurds surronding the area, though they don't speak much english, they make sure nothing wrong is going on. The beach is just as pretty and there are lots of palm trees for shade! Make sure you wear sunscreen! If you want to get a good seat, then be prepared to wake up early and put a towel on a chair, just in case. While in Punta Cana, i would go on at least one excursion. I have been on the Outback Safari and the trip to Saona Island, both of them were incredible! You get to have fun and learn a little bit about how life is like there. At night, the hotels have shows that either have dancers, or involve participation from the audience, which are funny! Overall, i would reccomend this resort to anyone! Have fun and safe travels! :)

<Author>ehiggins1505
<Content>Great Vacation My husband and I (both 28) stayed at the Barcel Bavaro Caribe March 5th ?12th. Overall we had a great vacation. We paid $830 USD each and felt it was well worth the money. I have paid over $1200 pp at resorts in Cancun and Cozumel and felt that the Barcel had much more to offer than those resorts. There were people of all different ages from all over the world. It was nice to have such diversity. The beach was gorgeous! We have been to several different islands/countries and the Dominican has the best beaches by far. We felt the Caribe was nicer than the Beach resort, however, there is a lot more going on at the Beach resort and therefore, more fun to hang out at. Both resorts are so close to each other, it really doesn matter which one you stay at. Be sure to visit the water sports building on the beach between the caribe and beach resort. We really wanted to go snorkeling, but the excursions they sell are usually all day trips. We were able to go on a one and a half hour snorkeling trip for $15 USD through the water sports center at the resort. The food was ok. I knew it was not going to be great, but there is plenty of it so you won go hungry. I liked the Italian the best and my husband liked the Mexican. The drinks were pretty good; however, I wish there had been a little more variety. If you are ordering a frozen drink, be sure to ask for alcohol in it otherwise they will not put it in. The mojitos and banana mamas are great. Also, if you ask, they will make you frozen drinks blended with fresh fruit and ice at the pool bars. If you don ask, they will give you slush from the machine. The cappuccino was also great. We went to the Casino and lost $50. The only other times we went there was for the buffet, although I really didn think it was any better than the buffets at the beach and caribe. Rooms are not great, but they are clean and have everything you need. We were only in there to sleep anyway. They have electronic safety deposit boxes which we thought was great. We went to the disco twice. They play good music and we had a great time there. The service was hit or miss. We were never treated rudely, but some people were better than others. Omar and Jhonf at the Caribe pool bar were outstanding! We didn take malaria pills before we went. Our travel agent said we had the same chance of getting malaria as we do west nile in the US. Overall, if you are looking for an inexpensive quality vacation, this is a great place. Keep in mind that you get what you pay for. In the end, you are in paradise, away from work, being taken care of, what more can you ask for?  
<Date>Mar 23, 2005
