<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great times I visited the Caribe from March 7th tot he 14th. It was excellent!! The place itself is beautiful- the beach, the gardens and the overall lay out. Here are a few things to note: I'm 24 and wasn't necessarily looking to party- which was good. There is a disco and the nightly shows, which are entertaining, but most nights people are quiet. (the disco played very current american music). Basically, don't go there if your looking to hook up and party all week. Best restaurants in my opinion? Beach Buffet, La Uva for lunch (my favorite- excellent service. try the fried squid and homemade croquettes), and the steak house. Best pizza is by the steak house as well (good fries). We went on the James Bond trip (little speed boats and snorkling). Very fun and worth it. The bad side? It is true that the rooms aren't excellent, although clean and decent. The people do speak mostly spanish. We had this one bar tender at the Casino beach bar be extremely rude to us and made fun of us in front of everyone. But mostly, a smile goes a long way and it isn't even necessary to tip. (Although it helps). Overall, I plan on going back next year.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Fantastic Resort We stayed at the Barcello Bavaro Caribe from March 7th to 14th, 2004.First off, the Punta Cana airport is great, basically on big grass hut.Our Signature vacations Rep led us to our bus and we headed of. The Barcello is one of the closest resorts to the airport, which is nice. When we arrived, there was some confusion over whether we were staying at the Beach Hotel or Caribe. Unfortunately the Signature Vacations rep wasn't there at the hotel. We got dropped off at the Caribe so that's where we ended up. Overall, I think the Caribe (which used to be called The Garden, is just as nice or nicer than the Beach Hotel. It has a great garden and it's a little quiter than the Beach hotel, but both the Beach and Caribe Hotels are the same distance from the beach and the views are basically the same.We felt that the food at the Buffets and restaurants were very good, the Mexican and Steak House were excellent, the Italian was mediocre at best. The buffets were good, great breakfeasts with fruit smoothies, and omletes made to your liking. We fellt the Casino buffet was the best and they made pasta and stir fry for you there. The pasta seemed better at the Casino buffet than at the Italian Restraurant. The seafood restaurant was very good, especially the shrimp and make sure to try the lobster at the Steak House, which is only served at lunch time. THe pizza seemed better at the Steak House take out.The drinks were good, but if you speak Spanish you may be able to better explain exactly what you want (mucho rum or pequeno rum). We took a Spanish dictionary to help us. Most of the staff don't speak much english. We liked the beer, fruit smoothies with rum and Pina Colada's with rum. You mini bar is stocked daily with Beer, Water and Pop. If you see the guy filling up the mini bars he will give you as much as you want. One thing though, the wine is terrible, almost not drinkable. If you want, you can buy bottles of wine from $5 to about $30 at the restaurants. Victor is a great bartender at the Beach Bar.The beach is great, lots of beautiful sand and topless women. The water is warm and relatively calm. We felt there were plenty of chairs, only a few chairs at the pool had towels on them (reserved) early, otherwise it was no problem. Since the Caribe is part of 5 hotels you can walk along way, the grounds are beautiful. You can also get around using the train.Other than the beach though, the extras are expensive if you want to para sail, etc.. but I guess that's to be expected.There are some good bargains to be found at the market, which you can walk to in 15 minutes. Be prepared to haggle and be hassled.The entertainment is fun, but you better like music and dance shows because that's what most of the nightly shows are. Get a list of the daily shows at your Hotel lobby. You can also practice dancing and fitness around lunch time.We went on an Outback Safari tour for $75 US. It was well worth the money. Our guide Luis was excellent. You get to see some culture and have some fun in the process.Overall the Caribe or Beach Hotels are truly 4 star. The Casino and Golf Hotels are a little too far from the beach so I wouldn't stay there unless you had too. If you stay at the Palace, you get more choice of restaurants but I'm not sure it's worth much more than a few hundred per person.Overall, we had a great trip and we would go back the the Barcello Bavaro Beach  Caribe.  
<Date>Mar 18, 2004

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Paradise on earth Four of us stayed at the Caribe resort from February 15 to 22, 2004. I would recommend this resort to anyone with no hesitation whatsoever. I would go back in a heartbeat. What a beautiful and peaceful place. The white sand beaches are beyond description. The beaches are exactly like the pictures. I would not have wanted to stay at any other complex except perhaps the beach resort. It is worth it to be as close to the beach as possible. If there is a downfall at all to this place, it would be the rooms. Don't get me wrong, they were very adequate and very clean and well kept daily, but I felt that they were in need of some renovations. But it certainly wasn't enough to bother me. We were only in our room to sleep. The rest of the time we were out enjoying the beautiful scenery and friendly people. The staff who work at the resort are so friendly and so quick to smile. They make life there even better. The food was good. The best place we found to eat was the buffet at the Casino resort. There was no end of almost any kind of food you wanted to eat there, and in my opinion it was all good. The mini pizzas at the Italian restaurant and the Steak House were really tasty. All in all, I would give this resort a big thumbs up. I don't understand how anyone could not enjoy themselves thoroughly here.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>loved it We spent a wonderful week at the Bavaro beach resort. We arrived at 12:30 am and were promptly given our room. The staff were friendly, the occasional bad one, no smile etc..but overall they were all nice. The cleaning service was great in our room, fully stocked fridge everyday. Leave a dollar tip and you will get great service! We got a chair everyday on the beach. If you want to sit near the pool, highly recommended that you get there early to place your towels. The Uva Grill on the beach is great to have lunch, just walk over in your bathing suit eat, then go back to your spot. The Italian and Mexican restaurants are good. Try the coco loco drink its excellent. Make sure you bring 1 dollar bills, I noticed that it was hard to get change for leaving a tip. You don't have to leave a tip, but we did because some of the servers were great and very nice. We went on the atv excursion it cost 50 per person, it was nice, but they could have given us more time to ride the atv. Overall the experience there was nice and I would go back.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Would never go back again. The trip consisted of two of my friends my girlfriend and myself, traveling form January 17 - 24th. We checked in around 1 AM, and were received by a skeleton crew that took way too long checking us in. Lets just say after hours of traveling we did not feel as though they were happy to see us. The topper was they strap a bracelet on you that made me feel like I was going to a bar for the night. You had to keep it on all week.  The room was very basic. There were two double beds a desk with a TV on it, two chairs and a table, one end table between the beds and a semi private porch with Wal-mart style patio furniture on it. The room also comes with a safe and a refrigerator. These two items caused problems upon our arrival.  You decide whether or not I am crazy or not, but I personally didn't feel very welcomed by the fact that our refigerator was not stocked properly. There were two bottles of club soda in there. NO WATER!!!! DON'T DRINK THEIR WATER! Also we could not access our safe until the next day. Seeing as though we did not check in for ten hours after the previous vactioners checked out I would expect that they would thouroughly go over the room, and make sure that these two problems could of been taken care of.  We've made it through the worst. As for the resort itself. The beach is absolutely gorgeous. Very large but if you want to get a beach chair head down there before you go to breakfast, and put some towels down on them otherwise they will be scarce. If you are a pool goer the same applies. The pool was awesome. The depth varied from 3ft to about 10ft. The was a large island in the middle with two small bridges attaching it to the outside. The same chair strategy needs to be applied here too. If you want one get there early, and plant your towel. Before I forget.... THERE IS NO POOL BAR!!!!!  There were plenty of activites as well that are included such as Kayaking, paddle boats, aerobics, dance lessons, and beach volleyball. Activites that are there but requires more money are snorkeling, windsurfing, air tours of the beach, and water skiing. There is also scuba diving which you do not have to be certified for. You can get training and 2 dives for $125 which is well worth it in my opionion.  There are plenty of other excursions on and off the resort. Horseback riding is on the resort. The horses difinitley know hwere they are going and move as they want but it was still nice. There is Golf at the golf resort. I cant speak for that since I am not a golfer, I can say that the miniature golf is very challenging, and was enjoyed by all. We also took the four wheeler excusion which was a lot of fun. My companions went ont he Jeep Safari last year, and said that was equally as enjoyable. You will see many things for Manatee Park. Apparantly do not go. We didn't go due to all of the bad reviews we got from our travel companions who went last year, and from some other negative comments made by people who did go.  OK back to the resort. The resort is actually 5 resorts bordering eachother. Now you can go to any of them. The beach connects most of them. You need passes to eat any any resort that is not the one your staying at.  This leads to the food and service which complemented eachother perfectly. They were both bad. First of all do not fall for the number of restaurants that are on the resort. We did only to discover that there were only 7 that were included in the All Inclusive package. Three of which are buffets which were quite unpleasant. The other four were barely average. My personal recommendations would be La Una for lunch which is at the golf resort, and either the Italian restaurant at the Caribe, or the mexican restaurant at the beach resort.  As for the service... let me put it this way. Ya better speak Spanish. This may sound silly seeing as though it is a Spanish speaking country, but I would think they would have a couple of bilinguals behind the bar or as servers. Very few. So I am coming from a point of view of someone who speaks very little Spanish. When you need a drink at dinner double up because if you get them to bring a round to you, your lucky. Don't look for a second trip. Service at the bar is not anything great either but it is much easier to get a drink there. (duh)  Finally I will end at the Casino and night life. The shows are entertaining. They keep the pace with most resort shows. (ie. newlywed game, dating game etc.) The are bilingual in the fact that he repeats what he says in at least Spanish and English. Theyare very high energy and will keep you entertained. The Casino is small. The have Black Jack, Caribean Stud style Poker, Roulette and Slots. The black jack is dealt differently the n in the states giving the house a slightly larger advantage. The poker is where I spent my time when I was in there. Enjoyable but left me longing for Atlantic City and Vegas.  The Barcelo Bavaro was a learning experience. Not all All Inclusive Resorts are the same. We will continue to go more mainstream resorts from now on. We did enjoy ourselves, but we take complete and total responcibility for that.

<Author>candiceozzie1
<Content>Cant go wrong with a Barcelo resort, great place From Winnipeg, Jan7-14, 2004Dont listen to the bad reviews of this resort it is great.We only found minor miniscule things that we decided to not ruin our vacation but you can decide if you want it to not. 1. Was that the staff seemed unhappy, at the beach, and caribe resorts. We found the best service and staff at the casino and golf bars. Nicest staff was Gerson at the casino pool bar. Otherwise the beach is amazing you can walk in either direction forever, there are no rocks in the water and they try to clean the beach dailyThe buffet seemed to have more selection at the beach hotel, but the pool is nicer at the caribe(used to be called garden) A la cartes mexican, italian and steakhouse were all great we like the steakhouse the best (not sure why others complained about it??) have the ribeye tastes jsut as good as at home. Rooms are standard, nice to have a mini bar stocked with 2 presidente beers, bottles of coke etc and water daily and nice to have a coffe maker.One note is if you walk down the beach past the palace hotel there is a little market also if you walk a little further there is a uy who offers camel rides. Overall you cant go wrong with a barcelo nice beach, nice pool, standard but still nice rooms, huge place with lots of bars, casino, disco, restaurants what more can you ask for??Oh weather was great as well, 5 mins of rain the whole week!
